./ci
  Run the same checks that GitLab CI runs, using Docker.
  Usage: ./ci

./fetch
  Fetch the latest changes for bare git repos in ref/ from Gerrit.
  Usage: ./fetch

./find_dependencies_minimal_bottom_up
  Find the minimum dependencies needed for a repository's Selenium tests to pass.
  Usage: ./find_dependencies_minimal_bottom_up extensions/Echo

./find_dependencies_minimal_gated
  Find minimum dependencies for all gated repositories (or a single component).
  Usage: ./find_dependencies_minimal_gated

./find_dependencies_minimal_greedy
  Find the minimum dependencies needed for a repository's Selenium tests to pass.
  Usage: ./find_dependencies_minimal_greedy extensions/Echo

./find_dependencies_minimal_thorough
  Find and verify the minimum dependencies needed for a repository's Selenium tests to pass.
  Usage: ./find_dependencies_minimal_thorough extensions/Echo

./fresh_install
  Installs MediaWiki core (without running tests).
  Usage: ./fresh_install

./generate_example
  Generate an example output file by running a command and capturing its output.
  Usage: ./generate_example examples/help.txt './help'

./generate_examples
  Regenerate example output files in examples/ by iterating each project-root script's # Usage: block.
  Usage: ./generate_examples

./help
  List all scripts with their description and usage.
  Usage: ./help

./install
  Installs an extension or skin (and its dependencies) into an existing MediaWiki core.
  Usage: ./install extensions/Echo

./install_all_gated
  Install all gated extensions and skins into a single MediaWiki.
  Usage: ./install_all_gated

./install_each_gated
  Install each gated extension or skin into its own fresh MediaWiki, one at a time.
  Usage: ./install_each_gated

./lint
  Run shellcheck on all shell scripts in the repo.
  Usage: ./lint

./list_dependencies
  Output dependencies for an extension or skin.
  Usage: ./list_dependencies extensions/Echo

./list_dependencies_combinations
  Output all possible combinations of dependencies for an extension or skin.
  Usage: ./list_dependencies_combinations extensions/Echo

./list_dependencies_optional
  Output optional dependencies for an extension or skin.
  Usage: ./list_dependencies_optional extensions/Echo

./list_dependencies_required
  Output required dependencies for an extension or skin from its extension.json or skin.json.
  Usage: ./list_dependencies_required extensions/Echo

./list_gated
  Output the list of gated repositories (extensions and skins).
  Usage: ./list_gated

./prepare
  Prepare the local environment for running Quibble.
  Usage: ./prepare

./prepare_gated
  Clone or fetch bare repos for all gated repositories.
  Usage: ./prepare_gated

./remove
  Remove src/ (MediaWiki source code).
  Usage: ./remove

./remove_all
  Remove everything quibble-local created, leaving only the git repo itself.
  Usage: ./remove_all

./remove_srcs
  Remove all src directories across all environments.
  Usage: ./remove_srcs

./restore
  Restore src/ from a previously saved state (created by ./save).
  Usage: ./restore

./run_php_unit_tests
  Run PHPUnit tests. Skips installation (assumes ./fresh_install or ./install has been run first).
  Usage: ./run_php_unit_tests

./run_selenium_tests
  Run Selenium tests. Skips installation (assumes ./fresh_install or ./install has been run first).
  Usage: ./run_selenium_tests

./run_selenium_tests_all_gated
  Run Selenium tests for core and all gated repositories (or a single component).
  Usage: ./run_selenium_tests_all_gated

./run_selenium_tests_gated
  Install all gated extensions and skins into a single MediaWiki, then run all Selenium tests.
  Usage: ./run_selenium_tests_gated

./run_selenium_tests_required_gated
  Run Selenium tests for all gated repositories (or a single component) using only required dependencies.
  Usage: ./run_selenium_tests_required_gated

./save
  Save the current state of src/ (MediaWiki installation) for fast restore later.
  Usage: ./save

./selenium_tests_exist
  Check if a component has Selenium tests.
  Usage: ./selenium_tests_exist

./shellto
  Open a shell in the container with MediaWiki running.
  Usage: ./shellto

./suggest_parallel
  Suggest the number of parallel workers for batch scripts.
  Usage: ./suggest_parallel

./test_integration
  Run fast integration tests and report which ones passed or failed.
  Usage: ./test_integration

./test_integration_slow
  Run integration tests that are too slow for the fast suite (./test_integration).
  Usage: ./test_integration_slow

./test_unit
  Run Bats unit tests.
  Usage: ./test_unit

========================================
= Running: ./help install 2026-05-26 18:50:31 UTC
========================================
./install

  
  Installs an extension or skin (and its dependencies) into an existing MediaWiki core.
  Skips core installation (assumes ./fresh_install has already installed core).
  Run ./shellto afterwards to open a shell with MediaWiki running.
  
  Usage: ./install extensions/Echo
         ./install skins/MinervaNeue
         ENVIRONMENT=0 ./install extensions/Echo
         VERBOSE=1 ./install extensions/Echo
         QUIBBLE_DEPS="" ./install extensions/Echo                    # no dependencies
         QUIBBLE_DEPS="EventLogging" ./install extensions/Echo        # only specific dependencies
         DRY_RUN=1 ./install extensions/Echo                          # pass --dry-run to Quibble (no real install)
         RESOLVE_REQUIRES=0 ./install extensions/Echo                 # install only QUIBBLE_DEPS; do not auto-resolve transitive requires
  
  QUIBBLE_DEPS: Override which dependencies to install (space-separated). When set, replaces
                the dependencies from zuul/dependencies.yaml. Set to empty string for no
                dependencies.
  
  RESOLVE_REQUIRES: Default 1. When 1, passes --resolve-requires to Quibble so it resolves
                    and installs transitive dependencies from each repo's extension.json/skin.json
                    "requires" field. Set to 0 to install exactly the deps listed in QUIBBLE_DEPS
                    (used by find_dependencies_minimal_* scripts for honest minimization).
  
  See: https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Selenium/How-to/Run_tests_targeting_Quibble#Install_MediaWiki_Core_and_an_Extension
  
(0s)
